Glanders_NNS and_CC Farcy_NNP ._.
THE_DT following_JJ notes_NNS have_VBP been_VBN compiled_VBN to_TO assist_VB horse_NN owners_NNS and_CC others_NNS in_IN appreciating_VBG the_DT importance_NN of_IN glanders_NNS and_CC farcy_NN and_CC to_TO facilitate_VB diagnosis_NN and_CC preventive_JJ treatment_NN of_IN cases_NNS ._.
NATURE_NNP OF_NNP DISEASE_NNP ._.
It_PRP should_MD be_VB clearly_RB understood_JJ that_IN although_IN the_DT words_NNS glanders_NNS and_CC farcy_NN (_( vernacular_JJ :_: penus_NN and_CC phuria_NN )_) may_MD be_VB commonly_RB used_VBN as_IN if_IN to_TO define_VB two_CD diseases_NNS ,_, both_DT terms_NNS signify_VBP the_DT same_JJ disease_NN ._.
Modern_JJ science_NN has_VBZ proved_VBN the_DT diseases_NNS to_TO be_VB the_DT same_JJ ,_, though_IN the_DT symptoms_NNS are_VBP different_JJ ._.
Glanders_NNS is_VBZ a_DT disease_NN of_IN equines_NNS (_( horses_NNS ,_, donkeys_NNS ,_, mules_NNS )_) which_WDT may_MD be_VB communicated_VBN to_TO some_DT other_JJ animals_NNS such_JJ as_IN dogs_NNS ,_, goats_NNS ,_, guinea-pigs_NNS ,_, and_CC to_TO man_NN ._.
It_PRP is_VBZ caused_VBN by_IN a_DT micro-_JJ scopically_RB small_JJ parasite_NN called_VBD the_DT Bacillus_NNP mallei_NN ._.
In_IN this_DT country_NN ,_, Glanders_NNP generally_RB assumes_VBZ a_DT chronic_JJ form_NN ,_, that_WDT is_VBZ to_TO say_VB ,_, it_PRP develops_VBZ slowly_RB ._.
Animals_NNS may_MD be_VB apparently_RB healthy_JJ for_IN a_DT long_JJ time_NN after_IN they_PRP have_VBP become_VBN infected_VBN ;_: they_PRP may_MD spread_VB the_DT disease_NN to_TO others_NNS without_IN themselves_PRP being_VBG suspected_VBN ._.
Sooner_NNP or_CC later_RB the_DT disease_NN becomes_VBZ more_RBR active_JJ in_IN the_DT animal_NN 's_POS system_NN ,_, and_CC the_DT patient_NN presents_VBZ certain_JJ clinical_JJ (_( visible_JJ )_) symptoms_NNS which_WDT will_MD be_VB described_VBN below_IN ._.
It_PRP is_VBZ exceptional_JJ that_IN a_DT case_NN of_IN Glanders_NNS can_MD be_VB in_IN a_DT stable_JJ amid_IN other_JJ occupants_NNS ,_, and_CC that_IN they_PRP remain_VBP free_JJ from_IN contamination_NN ._.
Some_DT are_VBP almost_RB certain_JJ to_TO become_VB glandered_JJ (_( or_CC farcied_VBN )_) in_IN their_PRP$ turn_NN ._.
The_DT symptoms_NNS of_IN Glanders_NNP may_MD appear_VB and_CC gradually_RB pass_VB away_RB ,_, the_DT patient_NN may_MD resume_VB work_NN ,_, continue_VB without_IN symptoms_NNS for_IN months_NNS ,_, and_CC again_RB give_JJ indications_NNS of_IN the_DT disease_NN ._.
The_DT old_JJ and_CC debilitated_VBN are_VBP more_RBR prone_JJ to_TO suffer_VB from_IN the_DT disease_NN than_IN the_DT young_JJ and_CC vigorous_JJ ._.
MODE_NNP OF_NNP ACCESS_NNP ._.
Glanders_NNS spreads_NNS from_IN stable_JJ to_TO stable_VB in_IN two_CD ways_NNS :_: (_( a_DT )_) by_IN the_DT introduction_NN of_IN an_DT infected_JJ horse_NN ;_: (_( b_NN )_) by_IN the_DT infection_NN of_IN one_CD of_IN the_DT stud_NN by_IN some_DT external_JJ agency_NN ._.
The_DT germ_NN which_WDT causes_VBZ the_DT disease_NN is_VBZ found_VBN in_IN the_DT discharges_NNS of_IN infected_JJ animals_NNS ,_, especially_RB in_IN the_DT nasal_NN discharges_VBZ ._.
Any_DT means_VBZ which_WDT will_MD convey_VB the_DT germs_NNS from_IN an_DT infected_VBN to_TO a_DT healthy_JJ horse_NN will_MD convey_VB the_DT disease_NN ._.
Therefore_RB ,_, besides_IN by_IN actual_JJ contact_NN of_IN animals_NNS ,_, the_DT disease_NN is_VBZ spread_VBN by_IN means_NNS of_IN watering-troughs_NNS ,_, mangers_NNS ,_, food_NN ,_, pails_NNS ,_, grooming_VBG utensils_NNS ,_, surgical_JJ dressings_NNS ,_, &_CC c._NN ,_, &_CC c._VB Even_RB the_DT air_NN of_IN an_DT infected_JJ stable_NN is_VBZ not_RB free_JJ from_IN danger_NN ._.
PERIOD_NN OF_IN INCUBATION_NNP ._.
Actual_JJ experiment_NN has_VBZ shown_VBN that_IN symptoms_NNS may_MD appear_VB three_CD days_NNS or_CC more_JJR after_IN infec-_JJ tion_NN by_IN inoculation_NN ,_, but_CC the_DT usual_JJ period_NN of_IN incubation_NN seems_VBZ to_TO be_VB about_RB three_CD weeks_NNS ,_, although_IN external_JJ signs_NNS may_MD not_RB be_VB evident_JJ for_IN three_CD months_NNS ,_, or_CC even_RB three_CD years_NNS ._.
The_DT rapid_JJ development_NN of_IN Glanders_NNP (_( and_CC also_RB its_PRP$ spread_NN )_) is_VBZ facilitated_VBN by_IN any_DT debilitating_JJ influence_NN afrecting_VBG the_DT animals_NNS ,_, such_JJ as_IN bad_JJ stable_JJ management_NN ,_, had_VBD feeding_NN ,_, over-work_NN ,_, bad_JJ climatic_JJ conditions_NNS ,_, chills_NNS ,_, &_CC c._NN ,_, &_CC c._NN (_( 21_CD )_) SYMPTOMS_NNP OF_NNP GLANDERS_NNP ._.

Note_NN on_IN Sheep_NNP and_CC Goats_NNP in_IN Bombay_NNP by_IN Mr._NNP J._NNP W._NNP Mottison_NNP ,_, Deputy_NNP Director_NNP of_IN Agriculture_NNP ._.

The_DT Deccani_NNP sheep_NN are_VBP probably_RB most_RBS extensively_RB bred_VBN ._.
They_PRP are_VBP owned_VBN extensively_RB by_IN professional_JJ shepherds_NNS who_WP with_IN their_PRP$ flocks_NNS wander_VBP all_DT over_IN the_DT plains_NNS in_IN the_DT fair_JJ season_NN ,_, but_CC retire_NN to_TO the_DT higher_JJR and_CC drier_RBR grazing_VBG grounds_NNS in_IN the_DT monsoon_NN ._.
This_DT breed_NN in_IN flocks_NNS of_IN any_DT size_NN does_VBZ not_RB remain_VB healthy_JJ in_IN the_DT plains_NNS during_IN the_DT monsoon_NN ._.
These_DT sheep_JJ require_NN dry_JJ grazing_NN ground_NN in_IN the_DT monsoon_NN or_CC comfortable_JJ shelter_NN at_IN night_NN during_IN heavy_JJ rain_NN ._.
The_DT necessary_JJ shelter_NN can_MD only_RB be_VB arranged_VBN for_IN with_IN small_JJ flocks_NNS ._.
Sheep_NNP owned_VBN by_IN villagers_NNS are_VBP sheltered_VBN in_IN the_DT houses_NNS or_CC out-houses_NNS ,_, but_CC each_DT owner_NN has_VBZ only_RB a_DT very_RB few_JJ sheep_NN ._.
The_DT Deccani_NNP sheep_NN are_VBP of_IN all_DT colours_NNS ,_, many_JJ black_JJ ,_, some_DT brown_NN ,_, some_DT with_IN broken_JJ colours_NNS and_CC few_JJ white_JJ ._.
The_DT wool_NN is_VBZ coarse_JJ and_CC hairy_NN ,_, the_DT fleece_NN light_NN ._.
